creature vain bred requireth nourishment man alone hath giuen criyng weepyng teares whereby declareth want maketh signe would haue thing darkly knoweth yea onely doeth make hymself ready receiue food often refuseth offered hym brought vp many thousande lettes many daungers many kindes intrapmentes declare hard hym passe race life come fatalle ende whiche drawe furthe order make rehersall thereof bee harde neadles specially thyng knowne muche verie barbars liuing creature daunger mo disease none standeth hazarde priuie ambushmentes doth man lion wildnes yet doe one encountre serpent stingeth serpent man woulfe man whose hand daily receiueth muche harme furthermore none couetous none ambicious none vncontentable desire thinges onely incontinuall pain wearied calamity whiche euilles although thou perswadest thy self haue discomfited one two thinkest thy self sauetie yet thou must abide sore conflicte nature self seyng thou art enforced feare euen lightnyng element steche yearth scorpion stroke many kyndes poison venime whiche although thei neuer chaunce vnto thee yet fleshelice flea crablice many like vermines shall noie thee declare man daunger many thousande kindes misery also ye necessitie death moch cou ted vpo seyng indifferent well thinges liuing creature whatsoeuer borne must die retourne dust whence beginning wer kinde death fallen whiche came synne whereby also haue founde beginnyng life liuyng thing decaieth vniuersally hole sauyngthe death synner godlie liuer bee farre vnlike man alone whose onely bodie perisheth soule seuered continewyng euerlastyngly thei finder thereby voide suspicion albeit man euer yet ruled worlde founde certaine felowmates whiche would misconstre finde fault doinges clearer man conscience isthe nature good il reporter soner despise good mennes reporte neuer neadeth cast feare good men alway take good thinges good parte tullie saieth better man lesse dooeth suspect euill contrariwise euill speake well measureth al menne common iester wherewith maie peraduenture tyme set countenaunce matter ende shall bee laughed scorne vaine bragge ape bee ape still saith luciane although weare golden coat therefore standeth soche goodes vice hoorehuntyng glotonie dronkennesse soche viciousagainst soch olde wretch glorie former meanes whiche although haue left olde accustomed vice yet either remorse conscienc weaknesse bodie wherein mena brasen bull deuised p lari men put tormented might bee tormented made hote thende pain thei might bellowe like beastes crie like menne moue execucioner pitie yet poincts cruell caused chief men citee flaine whiche ensamples although thei bee wonderfull monstruous worthie come mannes knowledge yet thei left vnto v writyng without goddes prouidence thei mighte terrour prince magistrate thei attempte like perswade themselues bee men thei ought affectate nothing malike atteptes thei might tourne gouernement people destruction owne commoditie honour countrey glorie god men reuerenzed onely maiestie also humanitie howbeit meane sotuer woulues dooe endenour chaunge heare woulle like vertumnus transforme theimselues sondrie shape yet thei chaunge nature burste disclose mynde asno longe co midas bewraied eares whereby came also passe men thei could lenger abide vilanie contempt wronge insolencie seruile yoke thoughte beste one shake feare make ende soche odious dominacion deuise soche successe hath ben one tiraunte whiche hath miserable ende bicause people hath wicked hath escaped reuengement hand yet hath died soche death hath gratefull wished men moste
